< text>
My rear shifter cable snapped on my Trek Domane 5.2 after about 6000 miles of riding.  I also took the bike in for a full clean and tuneup with their ultra clean package. < Review>
T & T Liberty Safe is a quality, reputable, knowledgeable and friendly business in my town (and other locations). My wife and I recently purchased a Fatboy Jr safe during their "no tax sale". They held it until I was ready for delivery. I called for delivery and they came out the next day! That is probably not typical, but it worked for me. The delivery/install guys were prompt, courteous and quick- in and out less than 1 hour including bolting it down. It fit perfectly in a closet with room to hide it behind doors or a curtain. They set up the interior lights and our password/combinations. The safe is a really cool dark green marble exterior with a clean interior including fully adjustable shelves. < review>
I started my dental cleanings after I moved to California . I chose western dental primarily because they were close to my home.
Since I began i have seen 4 different dentists no explanation given. In January I needed a tooth removed and was given a contract for a implant. I paid the uninsured balance on the spot. Thinking that was it. After my wait period for the graft to heal I scheduled an appointment to have the rest of the procedure done. When I arrived no one seemed to know what was i there for they had my scheduled appointment as an emergency check in. Oh and another new dentist. After I was seen by the new dentist.  I was presented with a new contract for impression and crown. My original contract apparently did not include this hum
So I compare this to a contractor installing a set of cabinets then coming back a saying oh my estimate did not include doors or drawers .
When I first asked about my contract before I signed it I was told it was for the entire treatment for this one tooth.
Iam absolutely disgusted with the lack of concern for patients and ther inability to know what is going on with each individual.
The wait times are 1hr to 1.5 hrs after scheduled appointment just to see the dentist not very efficient.
